[0m12:30:04.220392 [debug] [MainThread]: On master: /* {"app": "dbt", "dbt_version": "1.9.4", "profile_name": "dbt_project", "target_name": "dev", "connection_name": "master"} */
with relation as (
        select
            pg_rewrite.ev_class as class,
            pg_rewrite.oid as id
        from pg_rewrite
    ),
    class as (
        select
            oid as id,
            relname as name,
            relnamespace as schema,
            relkind as kind
        from pg_class
    ),
    dependency as (
        select distinct
            pg_depend.objid as id,
            pg_depend.refobjid as ref
        from pg_depend
    ),
    schema as (
        select
            pg_namespace.oid as id,
            pg_namespace.nspname as name
        from pg_namespace
        where nspname != 'information_schema' and nspname not like 'pg\_%'
    ),
    referenced as (
        select
            relation.id AS id,
            referenced_class.name ,
            referenced_class.schema ,
            referenced_class.kind
        from relation
        join class as referenced_class on relation.class=referenced_class.id
        where referenced_class.kind in ('r', 'v', 'm')
    ),
    relationships as (
        select
            referenced.name as referenced_name,
            referenced.schema as referenced_schema_id,
            dependent_class.name as dependent_name,
            dependent_class.schema as dependent_schema_id,
            referenced.kind as kind
        from referenced
        join dependency on referenced.id=dependency.id
        join class as dependent_class on dependency.ref=dependent_class.id
        where
            (referenced.name != dependent_class.name or
             referenced.schema != dependent_class.schema)
    )

    select
        referenced_schema.name as referenced_schema,
        relationships.referenced_name as referenced_name,
        dependent_schema.name as dependent_schema,
        relationships.dependent_name as dependent_name
    from relationships
    join schema as dependent_schema on relationships.dependent_schema_id=dependent_schema.id
    join schema as referenced_schema on relationships.referenced_schema_id=referenced_schema.id
    group by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name
    order by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name;

  create view "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."demographic_stg__dbt_tmp"
    
    
  as (
    WITH demographic_stg AS (
  SELECT 
    "AGE",
    CASE
        WHEN "RACE"=1 THEN 'White'
        WHEN "RACE"=2 THEN 'African_American_Black'
        WHEN "RACE"=3 THEN 'American_Indian_or_Alaska_Native'
        WHEN "RACE"=4 THEN 'Asian'
        WHEN "RACE"=5 THEN 'Native_Hawaiian_or_Other_Pacific_Islander'
        WHEN "RACE"=6 THEN 'Two_or_more_races'
    END AS RACE_CAT,
  
    CASE
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=1 THEN 'Not_Hispanic'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=2 THEN 'HISPANIC'
    END AS ORIGIN_CAT,
  
    CASE 
        WHEN "SEX"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "SEX"=1 THEN 'Male' 
        WHEN "sex"=2 THEN 'Female'
    END AS SEX_CAT,
  
    "ESTIMATESBASE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2021", 
    "POPESTIMATE2022", 
    "POPESTIMATE2023"
  FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction" ## for folks interested in running this outside of the <REDACTED> process - you can replace with "Population_Predictions", or whatever you decide to sent it to postgres as.
)
)
SELECT * 
FROM demographic_stg
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_rate__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH growth_rate AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "DIVISION", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        ("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2021_2020,
        ("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2022_2021,
        ("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2022") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2022", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2023_2022
    FROM 
        "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
)
SELECT 
    "REGION",
    "DIVISION",
    AVG(growth_rate_2021_2020) AS avg_growth_rate_2021_2020,
    AVG(growth_rate_2022_2021) AS avg_growth_rate_2022_2021,
    AVG(growth_rate_2023_2022) AS avg_growth_rate_2023_2022
FROM growth_rate
GROUP BY 
    "REGION", 
    "DIVISION";
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_trends__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    # prep for k clustering

WITH state_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2020") AS pop_2020,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2021") AS pop_2021,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2022") AS pop_2022,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2023") AS pop_2023
    FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
    WHERE "SEX" = 0 AND "ORIGIN" = 0
    GROUP BY "REGION", "NAME"
),

growth_trends AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        (pop_2021 - pop_2020) / NULLIF(pop_2020, 0) * 100 AS growth_2021_2020,
        (pop_2022 - pop_2021) / NULLIF(pop_2021, 0) * 100 AS growth_2022_2021,
        (pop_2023 - pop_2022) / NULLIF(pop_2022, 0) * 100 AS growth_2023_2022
    FROM state_totals
)

SELECT * FROM growth_trends;
  );

[0m12:31:54.475054 [debug] [MainThread]: On master: /* {"app": "dbt", "dbt_version": "1.9.4", "profile_name": "dbt_project", "target_name": "dev", "connection_name": "master"} */
with relation as (
        select
            pg_rewrite.ev_class as class,
            pg_rewrite.oid as id
        from pg_rewrite
    ),
    class as (
        select
            oid as id,
            relname as name,
            relnamespace as schema,
            relkind as kind
        from pg_class
    ),
    dependency as (
        select distinct
            pg_depend.objid as id,
            pg_depend.refobjid as ref
        from pg_depend
    ),
    schema as (
        select
            pg_namespace.oid as id,
            pg_namespace.nspname as name
        from pg_namespace
        where nspname != 'information_schema' and nspname not like 'pg\_%'
    ),
    referenced as (
        select
            relation.id AS id,
            referenced_class.name ,
            referenced_class.schema ,
            referenced_class.kind
        from relation
        join class as referenced_class on relation.class=referenced_class.id
        where referenced_class.kind in ('r', 'v', 'm')
    ),
    relationships as (
        select
            referenced.name as referenced_name,
            referenced.schema as referenced_schema_id,
            dependent_class.name as dependent_name,
            dependent_class.schema as dependent_schema_id,
            referenced.kind as kind
        from referenced
        join dependency on referenced.id=dependency.id
        join class as dependent_class on dependency.ref=dependent_class.id
        where
            (referenced.name != dependent_class.name or
             referenced.schema != dependent_class.schema)
    )

    select
        referenced_schema.name as referenced_schema,
        relationships.referenced_name as referenced_name,
        dependent_schema.name as dependent_schema,
        relationships.dependent_name as dependent_name
    from relationships
    join schema as dependent_schema on relationships.dependent_schema_id=dependent_schema.id
    join schema as referenced_schema on relationships.referenced_schema_id=referenced_schema.id
    group by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name
    order by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name;

  create view "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."demographic_stg__dbt_tmp"
    
    
  as (
    WITH demographic_stg AS (
  SELECT 
    "AGE",
    CASE
        WHEN "RACE"=1 THEN 'White'
        WHEN "RACE"=2 THEN 'African_American_Black'
        WHEN "RACE"=3 THEN 'American_Indian_or_Alaska_Native'
        WHEN "RACE"=4 THEN 'Asian'
        WHEN "RACE"=5 THEN 'Native_Hawaiian_or_Other_Pacific_Islander'
        WHEN "RACE"=6 THEN 'Two_or_more_races'
    END AS RACE_CAT,
  
    CASE
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=1 THEN 'Not_Hispanic'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=2 THEN 'HISPANIC'
    END AS ORIGIN_CAT,
  
    CASE 
        WHEN "SEX"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "SEX"=1 THEN 'Male' 
        WHEN "sex"=2 THEN 'Female'
    END AS SEX_CAT,
  
    "ESTIMATESBASE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2021", 
    "POPESTIMATE2022", 
    "POPESTIMATE2023"
  FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction" ## for folks interested in running this outside of the <REDACTED> process - you can replace with "Population_Predictions", or whatever you decide to sent it to postgres as.
)
)
SELECT * 
FROM demographic_stg
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_rate__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH growth_rate AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "DIVISION", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        ("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2021_2020,
        ("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2022_2021,
        ("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2022") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2022", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2023_2022
    FROM 
        "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
)
SELECT 
    "REGION",
    "DIVISION",
    AVG(growth_rate_2021_2020) AS avg_growth_rate_2021_2020,
    AVG(growth_rate_2022_2021) AS avg_growth_rate_2022_2021,
    AVG(growth_rate_2023_2022) AS avg_growth_rate_2023_2022
FROM growth_rate
GROUP BY 
    "REGION", 
    "DIVISION";
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_trends__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH state_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2020") AS pop_2020,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2021") AS pop_2021,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2022") AS pop_2022,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2023") AS pop_2023
    FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
    WHERE "SEX" = 0 AND "ORIGIN" = 0
    GROUP BY "REGION", "NAME"
),

growth_trends AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        (pop_2021 - pop_2020) / NULLIF(pop_2020, 0) * 100 AS growth_2021_2020,
        (pop_2022 - pop_2021) / NULLIF(pop_2021, 0) * 100 AS growth_2022_2021,
        (pop_2023 - pop_2022) / NULLIF(pop_2022, 0) * 100 AS growth_2023_2022
    FROM state_totals
)

SELECT * FROM growth_trends;
  );

[0m12:34:25.887069 [debug] [MainThread]: On master: /* {"app": "dbt", "dbt_version": "1.9.4", "profile_name": "dbt_project", "target_name": "dev", "connection_name": "master"} */
with relation as (
        select
            pg_rewrite.ev_class as class,
            pg_rewrite.oid as id
        from pg_rewrite
    ),
    class as (
        select
            oid as id,
            relname as name,
            relnamespace as schema,
            relkind as kind
        from pg_class
    ),
    dependency as (
        select distinct
            pg_depend.objid as id,
            pg_depend.refobjid as ref
        from pg_depend
    ),
    schema as (
        select
            pg_namespace.oid as id,
            pg_namespace.nspname as name
        from pg_namespace
        where nspname != 'information_schema' and nspname not like 'pg\_%'
    ),
    referenced as (
        select
            relation.id AS id,
            referenced_class.name ,
            referenced_class.schema ,
            referenced_class.kind
        from relation
        join class as referenced_class on relation.class=referenced_class.id
        where referenced_class.kind in ('r', 'v', 'm')
    ),
    relationships as (
        select
            referenced.name as referenced_name,
            referenced.schema as referenced_schema_id,
            dependent_class.name as dependent_name,
            dependent_class.schema as dependent_schema_id,
            referenced.kind as kind
        from referenced
        join dependency on referenced.id=dependency.id
        join class as dependent_class on dependency.ref=dependent_class.id
        where
            (referenced.name != dependent_class.name or
             referenced.schema != dependent_class.schema)
    )

    select
        referenced_schema.name as referenced_schema,
        relationships.referenced_name as referenced_name,
        dependent_schema.name as dependent_schema,
        relationships.dependent_name as dependent_name
    from relationships
    join schema as dependent_schema on relationships.dependent_schema_id=dependent_schema.id
    join schema as referenced_schema on relationships.referenced_schema_id=referenced_schema.id
    group by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name
    order by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name;

  as (
    WITH demographic_stg AS (
  SELECT 
    "AGE",
    CASE
        WHEN "RACE"=1 THEN 'White'
        WHEN "RACE"=2 THEN 'African_American_Black'
        WHEN "RACE"=3 THEN 'American_Indian_or_Alaska_Native'
        WHEN "RACE"=4 THEN 'Asian'
        WHEN "RACE"=5 THEN 'Native_Hawaiian_or_Other_Pacific_Islander'
        WHEN "RACE"=6 THEN 'Two_or_more_races'
    END AS RACE_CAT,
  
    CASE
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=1 THEN 'Not_Hispanic'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=2 THEN 'HISPANIC'
    END AS ORIGIN_CAT,
  
    CASE 
        WHEN "SEX"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "SEX"=1 THEN 'Male' 
        WHEN "sex"=2 THEN 'Female'
    END AS SEX_CAT,
  
    "ESTIMATESBASE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2021", 
    "POPESTIMATE2022", 
    "POPESTIMATE2023"
  FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction" 
)
)
SELECT * 
FROM demographic_stg
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_rate__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH growth_rate AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "DIVISION", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        ("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2021_2020,
        ("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2022_2021,
        ("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2022") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2022", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2023_2022
    FROM 
        "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
)
SELECT 
    "REGION",
    "DIVISION",
    AVG(growth_rate_2021_2020) AS avg_growth_rate_2021_2020,
    AVG(growth_rate_2022_2021) AS avg_growth_rate_2022_2021,
    AVG(growth_rate_2023_2022) AS avg_growth_rate_2023_2022
FROM growth_rate
GROUP BY 
    "REGION", 
    "DIVISION"
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_trends__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH state_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2020") AS pop_2020,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2021") AS pop_2021,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2022") AS pop_2022,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2023") AS pop_2023
    FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
    WHERE "SEX" = 0 AND "ORIGIN" = 0
    GROUP BY "REGION", "NAME"
),

growth_trends AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        (pop_2021 - pop_2020) / NULLIF(pop_2020, 0) * 100 AS growth_2021_2020,
        (pop_2022 - pop_2021) / NULLIF(pop_2021, 0) * 100 AS growth_2022_2021,
        (pop_2023 - pop_2022) / NULLIF(pop_2022, 0) * 100 AS growth_2023_2022
    FROM state_totals
)

SELECT * FROM growth_trends
  );

        "REGION", 
        "STATE", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN",

    from pg_views

    union all
    select
      'postgres' as database,

[0m12:36:11.161863 [debug] [MainThread]: On master: /* {"app": "dbt", "dbt_version": "1.9.4", "profile_name": "dbt_project", "target_name": "dev", "connection_name": "master"} */
with relation as (
        select
            pg_rewrite.ev_class as class,
            pg_rewrite.oid as id
        from pg_rewrite
    ),
    class as (
        select
            oid as id,
            relname as name,
            relnamespace as schema,
            relkind as kind
        from pg_class
    ),
    dependency as (
        select distinct
            pg_depend.objid as id,
            pg_depend.refobjid as ref
        from pg_depend
    ),
    schema as (
        select
            pg_namespace.oid as id,
            pg_namespace.nspname as name
        from pg_namespace
        where nspname != 'information_schema' and nspname not like 'pg\_%'
    ),
    referenced as (
        select
            relation.id AS id,
            referenced_class.name ,
            referenced_class.schema ,
            referenced_class.kind
        from relation
        join class as referenced_class on relation.class=referenced_class.id
        where referenced_class.kind in ('r', 'v', 'm')
    ),
    relationships as (
        select
            referenced.name as referenced_name,
            referenced.schema as referenced_schema_id,
            dependent_class.name as dependent_name,
            dependent_class.schema as dependent_schema_id,
            referenced.kind as kind
        from referenced
        join dependency on referenced.id=dependency.id
        join class as dependent_class on dependency.ref=dependent_class.id
        where
            (referenced.name != dependent_class.name or
             referenced.schema != dependent_class.schema)
    )

    select
        referenced_schema.name as referenced_schema,
        relationships.referenced_name as referenced_name,
        dependent_schema.name as dependent_schema,
        relationships.dependent_name as dependent_name
    from relationships
    join schema as dependent_schema on relationships.dependent_schema_id=dependent_schema.id
    join schema as referenced_schema on relationships.referenced_schema_id=referenced_schema.id
    group by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name
    order by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name;

  create view "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."demographic_stg__dbt_tmp"
    
    
  as (
    WITH demographic_stg AS (
  SELECT 
    "AGE",
    CASE
        WHEN "RACE"=1 THEN 'White'
        WHEN "RACE"=2 THEN 'African_American_Black'
        WHEN "RACE"=3 THEN 'American_Indian_or_Alaska_Native'
        WHEN "RACE"=4 THEN 'Asian'
        WHEN "RACE"=5 THEN 'Native_Hawaiian_or_Other_Pacific_Islander'
        WHEN "RACE"=6 THEN 'Two_or_more_races'
    END AS RACE_CAT,
  
    CASE
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=1 THEN 'Not_Hispanic'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=2 THEN 'HISPANIC'
    END AS ORIGIN_CAT,
  
    CASE 
        WHEN "SEX"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "SEX"=1 THEN 'Male' 
        WHEN "sex"=2 THEN 'Female'
    END AS SEX_CAT,
  
    "ESTIMATESBASE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2021", 
    "POPESTIMATE2022", 
    "POPESTIMATE2023"
  FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction" 
)
SELECT * 
FROM demographic_stg
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_rate__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH growth_rate AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "DIVISION", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        ("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2021_2020,
        ("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2022_2021,
        ("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2022") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2022", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2023_2022
    FROM 
        "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
)
SELECT 
    "REGION",
    "DIVISION",
    AVG(growth_rate_2021_2020) AS avg_growth_rate_2021_2020,
    AVG(growth_rate_2022_2021) AS avg_growth_rate_2022_2021,
    AVG(growth_rate_2023_2022) AS avg_growth_rate_2023_2022
FROM growth_rate
GROUP BY 
    "REGION", 
    "DIVISION"
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_trends__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH state_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2020") AS pop_2020,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2021") AS pop_2021,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2022") AS pop_2022,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2023") AS pop_2023
    FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
    WHERE "SEX" = 0 AND "ORIGIN" = 0
    GROUP BY "REGION", "NAME"
),

growth_trends AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        (pop_2021 - pop_2020) / NULLIF(pop_2020, 0) * 100 AS growth_2021_2020,
        (pop_2022 - pop_2021) / NULLIF(pop_2021, 0) * 100 AS growth_2022_2021,
        (pop_2023 - pop_2022) / NULLIF(pop_2022, 0) * 100 AS growth_2023_2022
    FROM state_totals
)

SELECT * FROM growth_trends
  );

  create view "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."percent_differences__dbt_tmp"
    
    
  as (
    WITH Percent_Differences AS
(
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "STATE", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        SUM(("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100) AS Percent_Change_2021_2020, 
        SUM(("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100) AS Percent_Change_2022_2021,

[0m12:36:56.711063 [debug] [MainThread]: On master: /* {"app": "dbt", "dbt_version": "1.9.4", "profile_name": "dbt_project", "target_name": "dev", "connection_name": "master"} */
with relation as (
        select
            pg_rewrite.ev_class as class,
            pg_rewrite.oid as id
        from pg_rewrite
    ),
    class as (
        select
            oid as id,
            relname as name,
            relnamespace as schema,
            relkind as kind
        from pg_class
    ),
    dependency as (
        select distinct
            pg_depend.objid as id,
            pg_depend.refobjid as ref
        from pg_depend
    ),
    schema as (
        select
            pg_namespace.oid as id,
            pg_namespace.nspname as name
        from pg_namespace
        where nspname != 'information_schema' and nspname not like 'pg\_%'
    ),
    referenced as (
        select
            relation.id AS id,
            referenced_class.name ,
            referenced_class.schema ,
            referenced_class.kind
        from relation
        join class as referenced_class on relation.class=referenced_class.id
        where referenced_class.kind in ('r', 'v', 'm')
    ),
    relationships as (
        select
            referenced.name as referenced_name,
            referenced.schema as referenced_schema_id,
            dependent_class.name as dependent_name,
            dependent_class.schema as dependent_schema_id,
            referenced.kind as kind
        from referenced
        join dependency on referenced.id=dependency.id
        join class as dependent_class on dependency.ref=dependent_class.id
        where
            (referenced.name != dependent_class.name or
             referenced.schema != dependent_class.schema)
    )

    select
        referenced_schema.name as referenced_schema,
        relationships.referenced_name as referenced_name,
        dependent_schema.name as dependent_schema,
        relationships.dependent_name as dependent_name
    from relationships
    join schema as dependent_schema on relationships.dependent_schema_id=dependent_schema.id
    join schema as referenced_schema on relationships.referenced_schema_id=referenced_schema.id
    group by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name
    order by referenced_schema, referenced_name, dependent_schema, dependent_name;

  create view "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."demographic_stg__dbt_tmp"
    
    
  as (
    WITH demographic_stg AS (
  SELECT 
    "AGE",
    CASE
        WHEN "RACE"=1 THEN 'White'
        WHEN "RACE"=2 THEN 'African_American_Black'
        WHEN "RACE"=3 THEN 'American_Indian_or_Alaska_Native'
        WHEN "RACE"=4 THEN 'Asian'
        WHEN "RACE"=5 THEN 'Native_Hawaiian_or_Other_Pacific_Islander'
        WHEN "RACE"=6 THEN 'Two_or_more_races'
    END AS RACE_CAT,
  
    CASE
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=1 THEN 'Not_Hispanic'
        WHEN "ORIGIN"=2 THEN 'HISPANIC'
    END AS ORIGIN_CAT,
  
    CASE 
        WHEN "SEX"=0 THEN 'Total'
        WHEN "SEX"=1 THEN 'Male' 
        WHEN "SEX"=2 THEN 'Female'
    END AS SEX_CAT,
  
    "ESTIMATESBASE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2020", 
    "POPESTIMATE2021", 
    "POPESTIMATE2022", 
    "POPESTIMATE2023"
  FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction" 
)
SELECT * 
FROM demographic_stg
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_rate__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH growth_rate AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "DIVISION", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        ("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2021_2020,
        ("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2022_2021,
        ("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2022") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2022", 0) * 100 AS growth_rate_2023_2022
    FROM 
        "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
)
SELECT 
    "REGION",
    "DIVISION",
    AVG(growth_rate_2021_2020) AS avg_growth_rate_2021_2020,
    AVG(growth_rate_2022_2021) AS avg_growth_rate_2022_2021,
    AVG(growth_rate_2023_2022) AS avg_growth_rate_2023_2022
FROM growth_rate
GROUP BY 
    "REGION", 
    "DIVISION"
  );

  create  table "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."growth_trends__dbt_tmp"
  
  
    as
  
  (
    WITH state_totals AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2020") AS pop_2020,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2021") AS pop_2021,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2022") AS pop_2022,
        SUM("POPESTIMATE2023") AS pop_2023
    FROM "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction"
    WHERE "SEX" = 0 AND "ORIGIN" = 0
    GROUP BY "REGION", "NAME"
),

growth_trends AS (
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "NAME", 
        (pop_2021 - pop_2020) / NULLIF(pop_2020, 0) * 100 AS growth_2021_2020,
        (pop_2022 - pop_2021) / NULLIF(pop_2021, 0) * 100 AS growth_2022_2021,
        (pop_2023 - pop_2022) / NULLIF(pop_2022, 0) * 100 AS growth_2023_2022
    FROM state_totals
)

SELECT * FROM growth_trends
  );

  create view "postgres"."<REDACTED>_<REDACTED>"."percent_differences__dbt_tmp"
    
    
  as (
    WITH Percent_Differences AS
(
    SELECT 
        "REGION", 
        "STATE", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE", 
        SUM(("POPESTIMATE2021" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100) AS Percent_Change_2021_2020, 
        SUM(("POPESTIMATE2022" - "POPESTIMATE2021") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2021", 0) * 100) AS Percent_Change_2022_2021, 
        SUM(("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2022") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2022", 0) * 100) AS Percent_Change_2023_2022, 
        SUM(("POPESTIMATE2023" - "POPESTIMATE2020") / NULLIF("POPESTIMATE2020", 0) * 100) AS Percent_Change_2023_2020 
    FROM 
        "postgres"."<REDACTED>"."Population_Prediction" 
    GROUP BY 
        "REGION", 
        "STATE", 
        "SEX", 
        "ORIGIN", 
        "RACE", 
        "AGE"
)

SELECT * FROM Percent_Differences
  );
